Inria Sans Light Regular (InriaSans-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'InriaSans-Light', Everything looks good.

Pass

Inria Sans Light Regular (InriaSans-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Inria Sans' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light' = NID 1 'Inria Sans Light'.

Inria Sans Light Italic (InriaSans-LightItalic.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'InriaSans-LightItalic', Everything looks good.

Pass

Inria Sans Light Italic (InriaSans-LightItalic.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Inria Sans' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light Italic' = NID 1 'Inria Sans Light' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Italic'.

Pass

Inria Sans Regular (InriaSans-Regular.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'InriaSans-Regular', Everything looks good.

Pass

Inria Sans Italic (InriaSans-Italic.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'InriaSans-Italic', Everything looks good.

Inria Sans Bold (InriaSans-Bold.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'InriaSans-Bold', Everything looks good.

Inria Sans Bold Italic (InriaSans-BoldItalic.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'InriaSans-BoldItalic', Everything looks good.
